instruction what and how to paste here:
1. open https://eloratings.net/2022_World_Cup
2. right click anywhere
3. "inspect element"
4. left click (on three dots) just next to "html lang="en""
5. click copy and copy element
6. paste here (can override this instruction)
(instruction can stop working any time when they change website just a little bit, so its like only for today.
if that happens, we must change reading method in code)
